Assalamualaikum & Good Day

Please take note of the following important dates :

* 15-16 March 2023
   ~ Online Compulsory Registration Period (for those who did not register during Online Pre-Registration period)
   ~ No penalty will be imposed if you register during this period

* 19-30 March 2023
   ~ Online Insert / Delete Period (for those who have done subject registration)
   ~ for those who have not register any subjects, you will be imposed late registration penalty if you register during this period

Please log on to MyUTM portal to do the process (don't forget to click the "Submit" button) and please inform your Academic Advisor to approve your application accordingly.

Thank you
